___


this is a all of the method in anomaly and there names the list is BIG so i recommened to use the search feature in your browser typically (Ctrl+F)

Not every script is explained any vague script has built-in documentation

## actor_effects
A comprehensive system for player-centric visual and audio effects. Manages post-process effects (PPE), HUD overlays (like gas mask cracks or blood splashes), and audio cues (breathing, impact sounds) tied to the actor's health, radiation levels, and equipment status.

## actor_status_sleep
Manages the actor's sleep deprivation and recovery system. Tracks "sleep" value, triggers debuffs (vision blurring, stamina penalties), and implements the sleep interface logic, including time skip calculations and health/stamina restoration upon waking.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| actor_status_sleep:actor_on_item_use | |
| actor_status_sleep:actor_on_sleep | |
| actor_status_sleep:actor_on_update | |

| actor_status_sleep:destroy | |
| actor_status_sleep:force_sleep | |
| actor_status_sleep:get_sleep_deprivation | |
| actor_status_sleep:load_state | |
| actor_status_sleep:on_game_start | |
| actor_status_sleep:save_state | |
| actor_status_sleep:test_blur | |
| actor_status_sleep:toggle_feature | |

## alife_storage_manager
Core manager for cross-level and global data persistence. Handles the serialization and deserialization of complex script data (like the `m_data` table) into the game's save files. Ensures that mod-specific states, quest variables, and player statistics are correctly preserved across game sessions.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| alife_storage_manager:CALifeStorageManager_before_save | |
| alife_storage_manager:CALifeStorageManager_load | |
| alife_storage_manager:CALifeStorageManager_save | |
| alife_storage_manager:STATE_Read | |
| alife_storage_manager:STATE_Write | |
| alife_storage_manager:__init__ | |
| alife_storage_manager:can_switch_online | |
| alife_storage_manager:decode | |
| alife_storage_manager:get_game_object_state | |
| alife_storage_manager:get_se_obj_state | |
| alife_storage_manager:get_state | |
| alife_storage_manager:on_after_load_state | |
| alife_storage_manager:on_before_load_state | |
| alife_storage_manager:on_game_start | |
| alife_storage_manager:on_register | |
| alife_storage_manager:on_unregister | |

## arszi_psy

## bind_smart_terrain
**Description:** Manages "Smart Terrains" (or Gulags)  area-based logic containers that assign jobs (logic schemes) to NPCs and monsters. It handles population capacity, job assignment (e.g., patrolling, sleeping, guarding), and logic switching based on time of day or other conditions. In this mod, it heavily integrates with the `warfare` system to track faction control.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| bind_smart_terrain:bind | |
| bind_smart_terrain:evaluate_prior | |
| bind_smart_terrain:try_respawn | |

## bind_stalker
**Description:** The main binder script for the "Actor" (player command object). It connects the player object to the game engine's event system, handling initialization (`net_spawn`), cleanup (`net_destroy`), and per-frame logic (`update`). It acts as the central hub for player-related callbacks and logic extensions (often via `bind_stalker_ext`).

## bind_trader
Manages NPC trader object binding and trade interactions. Handles `trade_perform_operation` callback for buy/sell transactions, coordinates with companion rows and dosimeters for trader UI, manages state via `trader_object_binder` (saves/loads trader states), and integrates with `axr_trade_manager.script` for NPC auto-trading.

| --- | --- |

## class_registrator
Centralized engine-to-script registration manager. Maps engine classes (e.g., `CActor`, `CAI_Stalker`, `CHelicopter`) to their respective script-side binders and server entities. Provides specialized registration functions (`cs_register`, `c_register`, `s_register`) to ensure correct object factory instantiation for both client and server components.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| class_registrator:c_register | |
| class_registrator:cs_register | |
| class_registrator:register | |
| class_registrator:s_register | |

## closecaption
Advanced subtitle and radio captioning system. Manages contextual display of character dialogue (story vs. generic), handles radio-style audio processing, and implements distance-based volume/visibility limits for captions. Provides a hierarchical color-coded priority system for different dialogue categories (NPC, player, objects) and integrates with the tutorial system.

## combat_restrictor
Rules-based combat exclusion and restriction manager. Defines zones where NPC combat is inhibited to prevent breakage of story events or NPC safety. Manages restrictor registration for specific jobs, provides functions to dynamically apply or clear combat blocks, and integrates with `xr_logic` to ensure AI complies with zone-based peace rules.

## dialog_manager
Central engine for dynamic NPC dialogue. Manages phrase priority, preconditions, and actions for "hello," "occupation," "information," and "tips" dialog branches. Implements priority-based phrase selection to ensure NPCs provide relevant and diverse information based on their knowledge (`is_told`), social rank, and faction. **Description:** A sophisticated manager for dynamic NPC dialogs. It handles the generation and selection of dialog phrases based on priority tables (e.g., for "Hello", "Job", "Anomalies" topics) and preconditions. It allows for modular addition of new dialog interaction types.

## dynamic_news_helper
Support system for NPC-to-actor information requests. Manages dialogue-based tips and hints triggered by world events. Coordinates with the news manager to broadcast context-relevant tutorials or world alerts to the player's PDA. *note*: this one ticks me off

## game_backpack_travel
Implements the "fast travel to backpacks" mechanic. Manages the requirements for travel (safe zones, combat state, weight limits), calculates travel costs or cooldowns, and coordinates the teleportation of the actor to designated stash locations marked on the PDA.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| game_backpack_travel:on_game_start | |

## game_statistics
Persistence and tracking system for player milestones. Records actor achievements, visited levels/smarts, kills, and interaction counts. Manages rank and reputation progression by monitoring game events and saving the accumulated statistical state across sessions. Integrates with the relation system to adjust faction attitudes based on player behavior.

| --- | --- |
| game_statistics:actor_on_achievement_earned | |

## item_device
Standardized binder for electronic devices (PDA, detectors). Implements `device_binder` class managing device condition (battery power), parent tracking, and first-update initialization. Handles NPC PDA registration for lootable profiles and persists battery levels for the actor.

## mob_home
NPC "home zone" behavior manager. Defines spatial boundaries (radius, home point) for NPCs to patrol or guard. Supports aggressive vs. passive modes and integrates with the gulag system to ensure monsters or squads remain within their designated territories.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |

| mob_home:reset_scheme | |
| mob_home:update | |

## mob_jump
Automated jump behavior for monsters. Orchestrates three-stage jumping logic: gaze alignment, wait/evaluation, and physics-driven jump execution. Provides a binder interface to enable scripted jumps for specific monster encounters or pathfinding overrides.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| mob_jump:__init__ | |
| mob_jump:reset_scheme | |
| mob_jump:update | |

## mob_remark
NPC reactive animation and sound system. Triggers specific visual reactions (gestures, animations) and audio cues based on environmental triggers or dialogue state. Manages NPC capture/release during animations and ensures transitions between idle and reactive states.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| mob_remark: | |

| mob_remark:reset_scheme | |
| mob_remark:update | |

## mob_sound
Specialized sound playback system for monsters. Organizes monster sounds into themes and manages efficient playback synchronized with animations. Includes cleanup logic for stopping all monster-specific audio when schemes reset.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |

## phantom_manager
Management system for "phantoms" (virtual psy-entities). Handles spawning, removal, and tracking of phantoms triggered by psy-antennas or anomalous fields. Implements `PhantomManager` to maintain population limits and clean up entities when zones are deactivated.

## post_combat_idle
NPC AI post-combat behavior manager. Prevents NPCs from freezing in threat poses or endlessly shooting corpses after a battle. Implements a randomized cooldown timer (`post_combat_wait`) that transitions NPCs from combat planners back to idle or patrol behaviors once threats are cleared.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |

## psi_storm_manager
The `CPsiStormManager` class is a complex system that creates a dynamic and dangerous weather event in the game, complete with visual effects, audio effects, and gameplay consequences for the player and NPCs.

**Description:** Controls the Psi-Storm and Blowout Emission) mechanics. It manages the entire lifecycle of a surge: the warning messages, visual/sound effects, finding cover for NPCs (`pos_in_cover`, dealing damage to exposed entities, and respawning artifacts after the event.

## release_body_manager
The `Crelease_body` class is a system for managing the cleanup of dead bodies to improve game performance.

Orchestrates the automated cleanup of NPC corpses. Tracks dead bodies and enforces a "stay time" limit, after which bodies are safely released from the a-life simulation to maintain game performance. Coordinates with `safe_release_manager`.

## restrictor_manager
The `Crestrictor_manager` class is a tool for controlling the movement of NPCs, which is essential for creating believable and immersive game environments.

Dynamic space restrictor and pathing manager. Enforces zone-based restrictions for NPCs, ensuring they avoid hazardous areas or story-critical regions. Manages the reset of restrictions when NPCs change jobs or squads.

## xr_abuse
The `CAbuseManager` class manages "abuse" in the game. In the context of S.T.A.L.K.E.R., "abuse" likely refers to the player repeatedly hitting or shooting friendly or neutral NPCs. The manager would track these actions and trigger consequences, such as the NPC turning hostile.

| Method | Description |
| --- | --- |
| xr_abuse: | |
| xr_abuse:__init__ | |
| xr_abuse:execute | |
| xr_abuse:finalize | |
| xr_abuse:initialize | |
